141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159664181;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">七、</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159664181;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12pt;">&nbsp;</span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">前言：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">《维权网：中国大陆在押政治犯、良心犯月度报告》是维权网信息中心每月对大陆当下发生的羁押未判、强迫失踪和已经判刑的各个政治犯、良心犯案例予以汇总、统计，最终编辑和撰写了这一最新月度动态报告。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">自本月度报告的第<span lang="EN-US">101</span>期起，本报告全新改版。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">同时，鉴于</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">中国人权捍卫者（<span lang="EN-US">CHRD</span>）</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">所属的</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">《中国大陆良心犯数据库</span></b></span><a href="https://tenchu.org/pocd/public/"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://tenchu.org/pocd/public/</span></b></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"> </span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">已将本网月度报告中所涉及的良心犯均全部收录，因此，我们从<span lang="EN-US">101</span>期起，将绝大多数本月没有动态信息的良心犯简历不再在月度报告里显示。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">我们仍将把在押良心犯名录附于报告内，读者可以根据姓名登录进入《中国大陆良心犯数据库》</span></span><a href="https://tenchu.org/pocd/public/"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://tenchu.org/pocd/public/</span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp; </span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">查询所有相关信息，非常便捷。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">《中国大陆良心犯数据库》不但收录了目前在押的这个良心犯、政治犯，已经获释、死亡的良心犯、政治犯也在此数据库中可以查询到。《中国大陆良心犯数据库》收集工作整理自<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月开始，于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日共收录良心犯资料共<span lang="EN-US">3338</span>人。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本报告主要关注的对象是所有在押的政治犯、良心犯——这里包括已被判刑的和羁押未判的——所有我们能够收集到确切信息的政治犯、良心犯。本报告竭力就包括汉、藏、维、哈萨克、回、蒙古、朝鲜、满等中国大陆多族裔政治犯、良心犯在内的信息进行收集、撰写和编辑，力求全面真实反映当前中国大陆政治犯、良心犯的恶劣的生存境遇。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">本报告为了便于人们查询检索，完全以良心犯、政治犯的姓名拼音顺序制作了完整的在押人员名录。同时，本报告仍对所有良心犯、政治犯的刑期进行了统计，羁押未判的也全部列于最后。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">本报告名单人员一旦取保候审、保外就医、无罪释放、回家监视居住、缓刑或刑满释放，都将从报告正式在押名单中移除，但其简历将显示于本期报告中。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">本报告每月不辍，期期更新，其中凝聚了许多义工、信息员和编辑长期以来默默无闻的辛劳和奉献。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">8</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年多来，本网一共收集、整理、编辑过的有较为翔实资料的人员名单及其简历超过<span lang="EN-US">3000</span>多个<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">这个数字里内涵着本网所有工作人员在高度风险下的巨大付出。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">本报告之所以能够按时定期发布，并且信息越来越翔实，这也得到了大陆许多人权捍卫者的积极反馈和支持。本网对所有提供信息的朋友，在此一并予以感谢。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">八年多如一日，本网持续不断地对中国大陆政治犯、良心犯境况进行总结和报告，是为了抗议谴责中共当局以超期羁押、拖延审判、虐待折磨、殴打等各种方式对良心犯政治犯施加酷刑，而在中共狱中被酷刑虐待折磨是被关押者要经常面对的严酷现实。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">本网坚信，外界坚持不懈的关注，将会给狱中受难者以精神和实质的援助！本报告一直对中共当局使用各种酷刑手段迫害折磨政治犯、良心犯的行径予以的系统揭露，业已引起了海内外各个方面的强烈反响。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本网一直在及时更新、统计最新讯息，每月末发布这月度报告，谨以此表达我们对所有失去自由的政治犯、良心犯的关注和牵挂。并以此，告诉全世界不要忘记这些为自由、民主、人权而承担苦难的人们。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本网认为，本报告的定期更新和发布，可以直接反映出大陆当下的人权概况——因为一个国家的政治犯、良心犯的境况是这个国家最重要的人权指标之一。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本网</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">以此</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">揭示中国大陆当下恶劣的人权概况与良心犯、政治犯的悲惨处境，力求唤起国际社会对中国在押政治犯、良心犯的记忆，并予以持续不断的关注和呼吁，直至他们获得自由。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本网认为，定期将良心犯、政治犯的姓名和境况公诸于世，是我们能给予这些受难者以实际而有效支持的一种方式。我们深知，没有比被人们的遗忘更令这些良心犯、政治犯感到绝望和痛苦的事情。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">因此，我们必须肩负起这项工作，乃至是使命。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">八年多的风风雨雨已经过去，未来的道路上还会有千难万险，但是有你们的支持，我们仍将一如既往勇往直前！<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">最后，本报告虽经本网信息中心认真核查，并得到中国大陆许多人权捍卫者协助，但仍因条件所限，无法做到适时、准确统计全部在押政治犯、良心犯信息，报告所反映的只是冰山之一角，仍然是一份不完全的报告，这需要我们的继续努力！<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">如发现纰漏之处和补充信息，敬请指正，并尽可能知会本网。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本网邮箱：</span></b></span><a href="mailto:wqw2011@gmail.com"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">wqw2011@gmail.com</span></b></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></span></p><p class="MsoListParagraph" style="margin-left: 36.0pt; mso-char-indent-count: 0; mso-list: l14 level1 lfo24; text-indent: -36.0pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;">一、<span style="font: 7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span></span></b><!--[endif]--><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本期报告概述：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">《维权网：中国大陆在押政治犯、良心犯月度报告》月月更新，是一份关于中国在押政治犯、良心犯的动态报告。此为第<span lang="EN-US">104</span>期。至此，本报告月月发布历时已整整八年多。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本期报告全文共计</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">4</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">万<span lang="EN-US">8</span>千字</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">。本期报告对上期报告的所有政治犯、良心犯名单进行了一次全面的逐一核查。获悉上期名单中</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">40</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">人已被</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">刑满释放或取保获释。并获悉有羁押<span lang="EN-US">2</span>人被判刑，<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人狱中有新动态，</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">同时，本期新增了我们又搜集的被刑事拘留、强迫失踪的<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人以及被判刑的<span lang="EN-US">38</span>人，合计<span lang="EN-US">41</span>人的名单及简介。目前，被本期报告录入姓名发布的在押良心犯、政治犯共</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">1728</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">人。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">为便于人们查询，《维权网：中国大陆在押政治犯、良心犯名单索引》为本报告名单的唯一索引。索引是以姓名拼音顺序排列（<span lang="EN-US">ABCDEFG....WXYZ</span>）。同时，本报告对所有良心犯、政治犯的刑期进行了统计，羁押未判的也全部列于最后。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><a name="_Hlk162569632"></a><a name="_Hlk162449568"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; 11.0pt;">、本月获悉上期名录中刑满释放的<span lang="EN-US">40</span>人的名单及简历<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">齐文伯、任鹏、桑噶蒋扬、史宗喜、王爱弟、<span _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">王爱忠、王蕾、<span lang="EN-US"><span _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">张展、<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">1</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">、</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">艾则孜•艾买提（维吾尔）</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：<span lang="EN-US">47</span>岁，新疆阿克苏地区维族教长。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月因皮山县一个村市集从事宗教教学活动，被当地公安局拘捕，同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月被判入狱<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">2</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">、陈娟：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">吉林省德惠市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，以有人举报为由，德惠市天台乡派出所和德惠国保联合绑架陈娟，并拘留十天，后陈娟被取保回家。迫害期间，因陈娟是做熟食生意，店铺生计需要她，家人着急营救，被德惠国保勒索五万元取保回家。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，德惠市六一零公安局国保大队将陈娟拉到德惠市民心医院检查身体，后又把她带到长春医院检查身体。当天陈娟被放回家中，并被告知称，关于她的所谓材料已递交到德惠市法院。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日被德惠市法院非法开庭，历时四十多分钟。当时没有宣判，称让陈娟回家等结果。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，吉林省长春德惠市法轮功学员陈娟被关押到长春“病监大队”。清明街与北安路交汇的长春市医院公安局设立的所谓“病监大队”，对外挂的牌子是口腔门诊，实质是迫害法轮功学员的黑窝，很多老年法轮功学员非法被关在这里遭迫害。现获悉，长春市德惠市法轮功学员陈娟已被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年半，仍被关押在“病监大队”。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"></span></span><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/4/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E5%9B%9B%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-436399.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/4/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E5%9B%9B%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-436399.html</span></b></span></span></a><span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，丛霞外出贴法轮功材料，被大连西岗区国保大队和西岗区八一路派出所抓捕。后丛霞被构陷到大连西岗区检察院，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月被庭审，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月上诉，<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月二审被维持冤判。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月初，辽宁大连法轮功学员丛霞被从大连看守所转至沈阳女子监狱，因大连疫情原因，至今不许探视。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span></span><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/11/26/%E5%A4%A7%E8%BF%9E%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E4%B8%9B%E9%9C%9E%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E5%9B%9B%E5%B9%B4-434060.html"><span &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、方宗菊：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1961</span>年生，湖北孝感市安陆市法轮功学员。因修炼法轮功方宗菊曾经被判刑两年。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，方宗菊在安陆市区讲法轮功被抓捕，被抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被安陆市法院庭审，多日后得知她被判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span lang="EN-US" _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">、郭秀海：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">福建省福州市永泰县法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1963</span>年生，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年五十九岁，是永泰县卫生局退休职工。她于一九九七年修炼法轮功。中共迫害法轮功后，郭秀海多次遭到骚扰、抄家、抓捕、关押等迫害。郭秀海<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月因讲真相被警察抓捕，后被长乐县法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日被劫持到福建女子监狱，现被关押在三监区八分监区，每月只允许消费一百元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span></span><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/6/12/2022-6-12.html#zip4"><span style="mso-bookmark: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">江苏南京法轮功学员，男，<span lang="EN-US">1954</span>年生。曾任南京水泥厂领导。一九九六年十二月，胡元勤开始修炼法轮功。自<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年中共开始迫害法轮功后，其多次被绑架、关押，甚至于<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。胡元勤因发放法轮功资料，于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日被南京市公安局江宁分局、东山派出所警察抓捕，随即被关押在南京市江宁区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月中旬获悉：胡元勤被南京市雨花台区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。<b 0pt;">：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">辽宁省锦州市凌海市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，锦州市公安局太和分局国保大队共抓捕了十几名法轮功学员，包括：张英玲（<span lang="EN-US">61</span>岁）、金晓梅（<span lang="EN-US">52</span>岁）、康桂云（<span lang="EN-US">70</span>岁）、刘玉荣（<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日获悉，辽宁省锦州市凌海市法院对这名老人下达判决，其中张英玲、金晓梅都被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元；康桂云<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元；刘玉荣、李淑芳、陈文学皆被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，罚金两千元。康桂云刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span></span><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/8/17/447768.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、<a name="_Hlk167832421">李凤兰</a>：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">（李凤岚）甘肃白银市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1955</span>年生，原是甘肃省白银市平川区财政局职工。一九九七年开始修炼法轮功。一九九九年七月中共恶党疯狂迫害法轮功，其屡遭迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，李凤岚被警察叫去白银法院，当晚被关押到白银看守所，随即遭逮捕。后李凤兰女士被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月后，于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被关押到兰州女子监狱。李凤兰在狱中病情恶化，癌细胞扩散，平川区公安局仍不许她保外就医。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">9</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、李洪财：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">山东省平度市人，平度市古岘镇山头村居民，青岛市即墨市大信镇“福顺废旧物品回收站”经营者，维权访民。李延香的丈夫。其妻子李延香因维权被山东平度市法院一审以“寻衅滋事罪”被判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，刑满释放；其妻子在出狱后因其夫妇二人继续维权抗争，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，夫妻二人都被平度市警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘、逮捕。目前李延香被羁押于青岛市第二看守所，丈夫李洪财被羁押于青岛即墨看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月获悉，其获刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月。</span></span></span><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/11/blog-post_85.html"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">广州中山大学退休教师，<span lang="EN-US">1961</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月出生，广西横县人，大学毕业，住中山大学南校园西北区。<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，因去北京上访，她曾被劳教<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，关押到广州市槎头女子劳教所迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月在家被海珠区公安分局及新港街派出所警察抓捕、关押构陷，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年底被海珠区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，被罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元。上诉后，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1961</span>年生，家住黑龙江省伊春市金林区，<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月份开始修炼轮功，后因修炼法轮功李秀云遭到当地中共人员的骚扰、抓捕、抄家、强行洗脑、拘留等迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，伊春市金林区奋斗派出所的警察闯入李秀云的家中抄家，并抓捕了李秀云和她的丈夫，后将她未修炼的丈夫放回。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日被金林区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月，距她被抓捕仅四个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">。信息来源：</b></span></span></span><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/12/18/453263.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、<a name="_Hlk167832610">刘春琴</a></span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167832610;"></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：湖南省株洲市法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1975</span>年生，原湖南省衡阳轧钢厂职工，一九九九年七月二十日，中共开始疯狂迫害法轮功后，刘春琴多次被绑架、非法关押，在看守所、劳教所、监狱遭受迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日被株洲市天元区公安分局泰山路派出所恶警绑架；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日被株洲市芦淞区法院秘密非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，勒索罚金五千元；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日被送湖南省女子监狱继续关押迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">14</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：重庆维权人士。刘富祥位于重庆市九龙坡区石桥铺正街<span lang="EN-US">202</span>号房屋，因为拆迁问题未与地方政府达成拆迁协议。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，刘富祥和儿子刘汗、侄女刘丽珺、朋友鞠小林在家中休息，被一群不明身份人闯入，将四人打伤打残，刘富祥和儿子刘汗全身多处骨折。随后四人被以妨碍公务罪抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日上午，刘富祥妨碍公务案开庭宣判，到法庭旁听出来的刘富祥的姐姐刘富兰哭诉：弟弟刘富祥被重判<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月、侄儿刘汗被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月、侄女刘丽珺被判<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年零<span lang="EN-US">22</span>天、鞠小林被判<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刘富祥刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">15</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">、刘金焕</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：广州市番禺区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1964</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月出生，毕业于广东省建材中专，原番禺水泥厂退休职工。<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日晚上，刘金焕往停在钟村优瑞厂附近的小车门把手上放了几份有关疫情的周报，遭监控拍摄。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，番禺区公安分局国保与钟村派出所出动<span lang="EN-US">4</span>台警车，对刘金焕抓捕抄家，并将刘金焕关押到番禺区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日被海珠区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span></span><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/4/%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E4%BB%BD%E8%8E%B7%E7%9F%A563%E5%90%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4-434358.html"><b><span 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/4/%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E4%BB%BD%E8%8E%B7%E7%9F%A563%E5%90%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4-434358.html</span></b></a></p><p font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">：大午集团集团总经理。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日凌晨，河北大午农牧集团负责人孙大午及其亲属并集团子公司法人等近<span lang="EN-US">30</span>人被警方突击抓捕。其后，包括孙大午妻子刘会茹等部分公司高管，被以“非法吸收公众存款”罪名批捕，而孙大午等其他公司高管以“指定居所监视居住”的方式被采取强制措施。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，河北大午集团此前被“指定居所监视居住”的<span lang="EN-US">7</span>位当事人家属，分别收到公安送达的逮捕通知书。刘平被控罪名：非法吸收公众存款罪、非法占用农用地罪、寻衅滋事罪。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日<span lang="EN-US">9</span>时至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日<span lang="EN-US">16</span>时，大午案经历<span lang="EN-US">14</span>天庭审后当庭宣判：刘被判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">95</span>万元；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。 <span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span lang="EN-US" _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">、刘荣仙：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">云南昆明法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年的<span lang="EN-US">85</span>岁的法轮功学员瞿月仙与<span lang="EN-US">75</span>岁刘荣仙，因为<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，陆大新（陆方兰）被吉林警察抓捕，一直被关押在看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，陆大新被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，已经转至吉林女子监狱迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年多来，公检法相关人员一直在构陷她们。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日左右，李保兰、齐文伯先后被开庭。李保兰被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，齐文伯被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，但在庭审判决后她们安全回家了。可在<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，她们被豆张庄派出所警察与法院执行庭的人，强行从家中抓捕到武清看守所关押。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">、桑噶蒋扬：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">1976</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年出生，四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州（简称阿坝州）红原县人，藏名</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: &quot;Microsoft Himalaya&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">ཟངས་དཀར་འཇམ་དབྱངས་</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">，藏族作家，藏文藏语维护者，中国藏族政治犯。自<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月起，因中共政府欲让汉文化逐步取代藏文化，遂在中国所有藏族地区开始全面推行汉化教育政策，期间，其家乡四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州红原县所有学校的藏文教学亦开始全面实施汉化教育政策；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日因其为保护和弘扬藏族文化而在网上发文指出学习藏文藏语是所有藏人的义务，完全符合中国宪法，遂引起四川省阿坝州当局的强烈关注和维稳打压，同年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，被阿坝州红原县警方强行带走，自此失联；后知被以“在社媒上造谣”为由刑拘、逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，其案在阿坝州红原县法院庭审，最终被以“分裂国家罪”秘密判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日；据悉，其家人遭恐吓，不得外曝任何有关其被捕遭判的信息，否则将受严惩。目前在四川省绵阳监狱（四川省绵阳市涪城区御中南路<span lang="EN-US">269</span>号，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">621000</span>）服刑。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/03/4_21.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/03/4_21.html</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">24</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、<a name="_Hlk167833076">史宗喜</a>：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河北保定市法轮功学员，又名史春来，<span lang="EN-US">1963</span>年生，河北保定市满城区要庄乡两渔村人。一九九九年修炼法轮功，却经常遭当地中共人员、警察的骚扰、抄家、抓捕、关押。史宗喜<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月被保定要庄乡派出所警察抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日遭河北顺平县法院庭审。史宗喜被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月初被关押到唐山市冀东分局第四监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">25</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、王爱弟</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：河北唐山法轮功学员。家住唐山市丰润区白官屯镇田富庄村。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，王爱弟被唐山市丰润区白官屯镇派出所人员抓捕、抄家，被抄走大量私人物品。时隔一年多，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，王爱弟被遵化法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金三千元。现今王爱弟被关押在何处，家属无法知晓。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">26</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、王爱忠：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">1976</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">年生，祖籍中国浙江省金华市，现居住在广州，广东著名民主人士，南方街头运动倡导者之一。王爱忠因长期致力于推动南方街头运动，受到广东警方高度关注。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，六四<span lang="EN-US">25</span>周年前夕，王爱忠被广州警方于家中采取强制措施，随后以「涉嫌寻衅滋事罪」刑事拘留，关押在广州天河看守所，<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日取保候审释放。王爱忠是近年来一直坚持发声的民主人士，其在<span lang="EN-US">twitter</span>上的言论一直被中共当局密切监控。此次被抓捕，很可能是因言获罪。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日中午有人打电话给王爱忠，称其车被刮，诱其下楼，将人带走。随后，九名警察到王爱忠家搜查，向王妻出示了搜查证，搜走<span lang="EN-US">29</span>本书，两台电脑，一部手机。随后，还将王妻传唤到派出所，询问王爱忠的交往及言论情况，并警告勿发声。王爱忠随后遭刑事拘留，后遭正式逮捕，关押在广州天河区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日获悉王爱忠案已经移送法院，等待开庭。</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王爱忠案原定<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日在广州不公开审理被取消法院无任何理由和解释。王爱忠案于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日 上午<span lang="EN-US">9:30</span>分在广州天河区法院正式庭审，当庭宣判，王爱忠被判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/05/blog-post_99.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167833189;"></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：女 ，北京西城区法轮功学员。王蕾因发放法轮功材料，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日下午其家被西城派出所和国保抄。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，王蕾北京西城区德胜门外派出所抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日二次开庭。后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，二审维持原判。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span></span><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/4/24/459144.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/4/24/459144.html</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span 11.0pt;">28</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">、<a name="_Hlk167833233">王立芳</a>：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">王复春的母亲。因竞选村长，原天津下辛庄村恶霸村长黄双来对村民王复春参与竞选恨之入骨，多次带领亲信打手到王复春父母家逼其退选，二老也曾多次报警警方不管。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日夜间<span lang="EN-US">11</span>、<span lang="EN-US">2</span>点钟，黄双来带<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人夜闯王国廷家，暴力威胁王国廷，不准其子王复春参选村长，与闻讯赶来的王复春及众村民发生冲突，黄双来等三人被殴致死。该案<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日一审，天津一中院将“聚众斗殴罪”改为“故意杀人罪”判处王复春、王国廷、村民衡庆杰死刑，王立芳被判<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年有期徒刑。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月王复春与衡庆杰死刑通过并执行。王立芳刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">29</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">、王敏：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">吉林省长春市法轮功学员，女。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日晚上，孙雪冰、王敏夫妻被长春市二道区杨家店派出所抓捕，被关押在兴隆山看守所构陷迫害。王敏被判<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月被劫持到吉林省女子监狱迫害。她丈夫孙雪冰被判两年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span></span><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/7/24/463365.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/7/24/463365.html</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">30</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、王藏：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1985</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日出生，原名王玉文，笔名王藏、“小王子”，云南省楚雄市人，先锋诗人，自由作家，影视编剧，独立中文笔会会员，中国自由文化运动成员，中国曾押政治犯。王藏曾于<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年底以“小王子”为笔名开始涉足网络诗歌习作，自此走上自由写作之路，并对极权文化予以批判。<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月，加入独立中文笔会，同年遭到官方威胁和长达<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个多月的监视居住。<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年—<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年间因积极参与“中国自由文化运动”签名活动，又在《自由圣火》网站发文并设专栏、在博讯网上开设专栏发表文集等，而被贵州省遵义市警方于<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月再次强制监视居住<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，荣获“<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>《自由圣火》写作奖”。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，正式启用笔名“王藏”，藉以表达“来生愿做藏人”的意愿。自<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年起，因其积极参与多项维权民主活动、广交民主正义之士，并创作、推出了大量诗歌作品以及行为艺术，曾被北京当局多次警告威胁并驱离工作室和居住地，给其家庭造成诸多困扰。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，因其在网上发布声援香港“雨伞革命”的打伞图片，随被北京市宋庄警方带走，其家被抄，之后被以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘于北京市第一看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，被北京市当局以同罪名正式逮捕，其罪由包括行为艺术和诗歌、文章，网上发布声援香港“占中”图片，声援郭飞雄，声援建三江被虐打人权律师，在网上祭奠林昭，关注藏人自焚事件，声援新疆维吾尔族学者伊力哈木•土赫提、法轮功问题、纪念“六四”及揭批文革等多项内容。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，被取保候审释放；据悉，其在被审讯期间遭受酷刑。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日早上<span lang="EN-US">4.30</span>分左右，被云南省楚雄市公安机关突然以涉嫌煽动颠覆罪由带走，一直无任何消息。后王藏及夫人王利芹二人均被以“煽动颠覆国家政权”罪逮捕，王藏于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日被拘捕，<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日被正式逮捕，王利芹于<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被拘捕，<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被正式逮捕，二人已经于<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月中旬被移送云南省楚雄州检察院审查起诉。王藏被羁押在云南楚雄市看守所。指控王藏煽动颠覆国家政权罪名案件事实基本上就是他<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年那次被抓捕出来后所公开的言论、接受的采访、书写的诗歌文章、以及行为艺术。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，代理律师经与云南省楚雄州检察院电话核实，王藏（王玉文）、王丽芹夫妇煽动颠覆国家政权案于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日起诉到楚雄州中级法院。代理律师认为此前楚雄看守所不当限制律师会见，已经严重违法。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，王藏（王玉文）、王利芹夫妇涉嫌煽动颠覆国家政权案遭延期审限，本案最后审限从<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日再延期<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日上午，云南楚雄州中级法院开庭宣判王藏、王利芹夫妇构成煽动颠覆国家政权，分别判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年、<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。王藏、王利芹均当庭表示不服判决，提起上诉。王藏刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日获悉王藏已入云南省第二监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/01/blog-post_76.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/01/blog-post_76.html</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">31</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">、<a name="_Hlk167833371">王志燕</a>：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1967</span>年生，山西省太原市法轮功学员。太原市半坡西街居民，迎泽区人社局职工。王志燕因坚持法轮大法信仰，曾多次遭当地警察及社区人员抓捕、拘留、骚扰，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日遭鼓楼派出所警察抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">212</span>日被太原市万柏林区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。王志燕上诉，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月被太原市中级法院维持原判。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源</b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：</span></b></span></span><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/3/30/%E5%B1%B1%E8%A5%BF%E5%A4%AA%E5%8E%9F%E5%B8%82%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E7%8E%8B%E5%BF%97%E7%87%95%E9%81%AD%E5%86%A4%E5%88%A4%E4%B8%89%E5%B9%B4-440681.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/3/30/%E5%B1%B1%E8%A5%BF%E5%A4%AA%E5%8E%9F%E5%B8%82%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E7%8E%8B%E5%BF%97%E7%87%95%E9%81%AD%E5%86%A4%E5%88%A4%E4%B8%89%E5%B9%B4-440681.html</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体;">32</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri;">、危美甜：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女<span lang="EN-US">, </span>广州市花都区法轮功学员 一九八六年三月出生，家住广州市花都区新华街，是<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年春开始修炼法轮功的。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年下半年，危美甜在花都区新华街附近张贴了几张法轮功不干胶，被监控拍摄。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，危美甜被广州市花都区公安分局国保和新华派出所警察抓捕，并被抄家，家里手机、电脑、<span lang="EN-US">U</span>盘、法轮功书籍等私人物品被抄走。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，危美甜被花都区检察院批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年年底，危美甜遭荔湾区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，勒索罚金五千元。危美甜不服非法判决，提出上诉。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，广州市中级法院维持原判。危美甜已经被关押到广东省女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-style: italic; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">33</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-style: italic; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">、吴风桃：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-style: italic; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">女，广东揭阳法轮功学员。一九六四年一月出生，家住揭阳普宁市流沙镇白沙陇村。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，吴风桃被普宁市公安局和大南山派出所警察抓捕，关押到普宁市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，法院到普宁市看守所宣判，吴凤桃被判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"></span></span><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/3/7/2022-3-7.html#zip2"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/3/7/2022-3-7.html</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">34</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、肖艳芳：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">湖北孝感市汉川市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，肖艳芳、刘义波、王四美、王庆、舒运兰等<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人到汉川市马鞍乡联洪村、天成村告诉村民法轮功遭迫害真相及避疫良方，被村民举报，遭马鞍派出所警察抓捕。第<span lang="EN-US">2</span>天，<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人因疫情原因被放回家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，汉川市公安局对肖艳芳、刘义波、王庆、王四美、舒运兰<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人下达「监视居住通知书」。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日肖艳芳、刘义波被抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，汉川国保人员到湖南长沙，将流落在外打工的法轮功学员王庆抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，汉川市公安局分水派出所警察在分水镇抓捕了王四美和另一名法轮功学员胡汉姣。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月下旬，孝昌县法院作出判决，胡汉姣、王四美遭冤判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，刘义波遭冤判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月，肖艳芳遭冤判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，王庆遭冤判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。肖艳芳刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">35</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、杨玉兴：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">原在临海市职业技术高中教美术。<span lang="EN-US">1990</span>年左右，因为校办工厂经营不善面临倒闭，杨玉兴就接手该企业，并迁移到自己位于凌海市（原锦县）南师范街<span lang="EN-US">5</span>栋<span lang="EN-US">10</span>号私有房屋内，办理了工商、税务、环保等手续，用于经营化学试剂分装。另据了解，杨玉兴的该套私有房屋为平房，房产证的建筑面积为<span lang="EN-US">130</span>平米，占地面积<span lang="EN-US">200</span>平米左右。退休教师杨玉兴一直守法经营，照章纳税。到<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年，临海市（原锦县）政府官员以城镇化建设为名，与黑社会合起伙来搞房地产开发，他们滥发拆迁许可证，以合法身份掩盖非为目的，通过人民法院在杨玉兴房屋地块违法实施强拆。杨玉兴不服政府官员搞房地产开发的违法乱纪行为，向有关部门举报此事，结果被公安带上手铐游街示众，房屋遭到不法强拆，至今没有任何补偿与安置。<span lang="EN-US"> 2008</span>年奥运会前夕，杨玉兴在北京的出租房子里被临海市的维稳人员跨省抓捕抓回，由公安以“涉嫌寻衅滋事”劳教<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月份，已<span lang="EN-US">70</span>岁的杨玉兴老先生，因为在北京邮寄反映地方政府违法拆迁行为，被抓回当地后被以“涉嫌寻衅滋事罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，退休教师的养老金和一切待遇全部被剥夺，当地党政官员还指使黑社会对其女儿进行恐吓。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，已经<span lang="EN-US">75</span>岁且失去养老待遇的杨玉兴老先生，从北京回农村老家帮助兄弟地里收粮食，被凌海市公安局刑警队的抓捕，在杨玉兴老先生抓捕后，凌海市公安局也没有给杨玉兴亲属书面通知，临海市检察院作出批捕时，凌海市公安局同样没有把逮捕给予家属书面通知，整个办案过程完全暗箱操作。后由凌海市法院电话告知其女儿，称该院以“寻衅滋事罪”对杨玉兴老先生判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">36</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、<a name="_Hlk167833686">张展</a></span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167833686;"></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：女，<span lang="EN-US">1980</span>年代出生，陕西省籍人，上海市浦东新区常驻居民，网络异见人士，公民记者、民主公民。硕士学位，毕业后即在上海谋职工作；因不满中共政府的政治现状，长期在网络平台发布批评“一党专政”、腐败滥权等言论，其做派活跃、内容尖锐而颇具针对性，故而曾多次被上海市警方约谈、传唤及威胁；自<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年以来，因其在微信等网络平台大量转发香港“反送中”抗议视频及文图资料，尤其是每天自己撰文发声，利用行为艺术等为声援香港举牌，随于<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日被上海警方传唤，自此失联，后知其被以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留，其父因受警方威胁，故对外拒透其具体信息；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，终获释放；据悉，羁押期间，其曾被两次做强制性“精神病鉴定”。此前被羁押于上海市浦东新区看守所。张展自<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日左右去到武汉报导当地疫情，一直在微信、推特、<span lang="EN-US">YouTube </span>等社交媒体平台上直播武汉的现场情况，并尽其所能地帮助受疫情影响的人维权。张展在武汉实地写了大量关于武汉疫情的真实报道。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日在武汉遭“强迫失踪”，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日被上海市浦东分局刑事拘留，被控罪名是寻衅滋事，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月遭正式逮捕。被起诉，其在狱中绝食抗议，身体状况极差。至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月，张展的妈妈说，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日视频中看到最大的不同是张展身体明显好了一些，也比较牵挂父母家人。张展愿意在监狱里面做一些手工。她开始自主进食，不再被灌食；以前因为长期绝食肠胃比较疼痛，现在肠胃有所恢复；她可以独立行走，不需要他人搀扶。视频通话<span lang="EN-US">20</span>分钟后结束，张展也请父母保重身体。现羁押在浦东新区看守所。<span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">2020</span><span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，张展女士案一审开庭，并当庭宣判，张展女士因言获罪被上海浦东新区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。</span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/02/blog-post_13.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/02/blog-post_13.html</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">37</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">、赵海军：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1966</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年出生，黑龙江省哈尔滨市人，法轮功学员，在押良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月因信仰法轮功，并与其妻等人为中共镇压、迫害法轮功到北京和平请愿，被当局抓捕，先被关押于哈尔滨双城市看守所，后又被送到双城区单城敬老院进行强制洗脑教育，期间因屡受虐待酷刑愤而绝食抗议，当局才不得不于<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月将其释放回家。<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月因前往北京为法轮功进行和平请愿，而被北京警方抓捕，并被关押于北京市团河劳教所，直至一年多后方予以释放。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日因其屡次控告迫害法轮功的元凶江泽民，遂被当地警方从家中抓走，并被以涉邪教罪刑拘，其家遭查抄。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日被双城区检察院转正式批捕，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日被哈尔滨双城区法院以“组织、利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”重判<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元；其不服上诉，后虽经哈尔滨市中级法院二审，但依然维持原判。目前在黑龙江省呼兰监狱服刑。据悉，因在狱中遭遇虐待，致其长期不能排尿而被强制打针。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">38</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、<a name="_Hlk167833769">赵林</a>：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">黑龙江哈尔滨法轮功学员，哈尔滨市轴承厂退休职工，现年已经七十岁了。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日上午，赵林在南岗区先锋路附近粘贴了一张“法轮大法好”不干胶，被南岗公安分局国保警察抓捕、抄家，抢走其家中法轮大法书籍。后获悉被判<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年有期徒刑，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">39</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">、<a name="_Hlk167868062">常昊</a>：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">云南省昭通市镇雄县农村的基督教家庭教会传道人。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，常昊被镇雄县公安以涉嫌寻衅滋事罪刑事拘留，家里的圣经、属灵书籍和福音口罩及手机电脑等都被扣押。在经过两次退侦后，后被起诉至镇雄县法院，获释前一直被羁押在镇雄县看守所。常昊是二级残障人士，并患有糖尿病。常昊妻子姚发珍患有甲亢和腰间椎盘病。常昊母亲已经<span lang="EN-US">86</span>岁，腿脚不好，家里需人照顾。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日下午遭羁押一年一个月的常昊获释回家。常昊出狱回家，令人欣慰。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/05/blog-post_15.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/05/blog-post_15.html</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">40</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">、张海</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：湖北省武汉市人，武汉新冠肺炎死难者家属，武汉退休老人抗议医改“白发运动”支持者，人权捍卫者。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年初，其原为中共解放军老兵的父亲因在广东意外骨折，为了报销医药费，其把父亲接回武汉动手术，却在医院感染<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年冠状病毒而病逝，因其认为父亲染病与医院未妥善提供防疫保护有关，若非当局隐瞒疫情，他也不会带着父亲回武汉医治，遂其因此控告武汉市政府、湖北省政府以及武汉市中部战区总医院，并要赔偿金人民币<span lang="EN-US">200</span>万元；后因武汉病毒夺去了数以万计人的生命，故其从最初只为其父发声追责，逐渐发展为也广泛协助其他因武汉病毒死难的同胞追责；为了避免今后此类人祸再次发生，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，其与众多死难者家属及社会公益人士连手共同组建了冠病索赔法律顾问团，以求通过司法公正使得疫情真实信息公开，并据此维权、协商获取部分抚恤金和丧葬费，不料却遭到武汉当局的不断骚扰和伺机打压；<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月，全国多地如武汉、大连、鞍山等城市发生上万退休老人抗议医改的“白发维权运动”，其中武汉地区规模甚大，<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日和<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，武汉上万名退休人员聚集在市政府前抗议，要求撤回同年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日正式实施的大幅降低医药补贴的“医疗新政”，随后即有多名示威者被抓；其因对武汉退休老人抗议医改的“白发运动”表达了支持，并在推特上转发视频，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，亦被武汉市汉阳区警方带走，后以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘，自此失联；<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日获悉，其被武汉市汉阳区检察院以同罪名正式批捕，后已被起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月开庭，后获悉其获刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。其一直被羁押于武汉市汉阳区看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="mso-bookmark: Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，本网获悉：被控涉嫌寻衅滋事罪的江西南昌公民张晓东案今日开庭宣判，张晓东获刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，其不服判决，当庭上诉。因其宣判，本地好几位网民都被打了招呼，不能去旁听。张晓东<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日被抓捕，已被羁押了近一年半。其被起诉书指控涉嫌寻衅滋事罪，而证据全是其在微信群、朋友圈、<span lang="EN-US">QQ</span>群里的所谓言论，是典型的因言获罪。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日上午<span lang="EN-US">10:00</span>张晓东的寻衅滋事案在南昌市青山湖区法院审理，张晓东坚信自己无罪。</span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: </span><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张晓东：</span></b></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US">1960</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日生。铁路部门停薪留职，下海经商多年，已退休。为人热情慷慨，好交友。每有朋友落难，包括本地公民朋友与律师落难，他都会奔走帮助。张晓东<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日被当地警方抓捕，随后就遭刑事拘留。后于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日被批准逮捕。张晓东与<span lang="EN-US">‘</span>江西九江四公民<span lang="EN-US">’</span>案被捕人员均为好友。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日被移送检察院起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日开庭审理。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。其不服判决，当庭上诉。目前张晓东现羁押在南昌市第一看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p lang="EN-US">12</span>，本网获悉：山东高密市<span lang="EN-US">71</span>岁的法轮功学员徐秀珍女士被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span Roman&quot;;">徐秀珍：</span></b></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span
