lang="EN-US">1953</span>年生，现年<span lang="EN-US">71</span>岁。家住高密市夏庄镇益民村，她与丈夫秦松法、大女儿秦少华于一九九八年开始修炼法轮大法。自<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月中共当局开始大规模迫害法轮功，徐秀珍一家也屡遭中共迫害，她与丈夫秦松法曾两次被判刑，大女儿秦少华一次被劳教、一次被判刑。徐秀珍老太太于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日被高密市公安局及夏庄派出所警察抓捕，关押在潍坊市看守所。随即遭刑事拘留，后遭批捕、起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月上旬获悉：徐秀珍被高密市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，目前已被转监到山东省女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2</span></b></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">朱玉芳：获刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年的狱中江西维权人士朱玉芳被江西省女子监狱停止了与家属的亲情会见和亲情电话<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，本网获悉：近日，被以“寻衅滋事”罪名判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年的江西维权人士朱玉芳，近期在其服刑的江西省女子监狱，被监狱方停止了与家属的亲情会见和亲情电话的权利，其家属无法探望，也无法与其电话沟通。与家属的亲情会见和亲情电话，是每个服刑犯人应有的人道待遇和权利，而监狱方却把这种人道待遇和权利，作为惩罚或奖励犯人的手段。朱玉芳在江西女子监狱的境况，亟需关注！<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/05/4.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/05/4.html</span></b></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">朱玉芳简介</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：江西萍乡的强拆维权者。曾是经营<span lang="EN-US">4</span>家店面的私营业主，<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年拆迁中，萍乡市政府主要领导亲属开办的房地产公司拒不兑现拆迁协议，朱玉芳被迫走上维权之路。在维权过程中，她不仅自己维权，也积极帮助他人维权，呼吁社会公正，遂被地方政府视为重点维稳控制和打击对象，被多次截访绑架、关黑监狱、遭受酷刑。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年，朱玉芳因在北京身穿“没有腐败就没有访民”的文化衫维权，被北京警方抓走，转交给江西萍乡安源区警方以“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘，后被萍乡市安源区法院以“寻衅滋事”罪名判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年出狱后，朱玉芳一直为被枉法冤判而申诉；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，她到江西省高级法院申诉，遭拒，遂在法院门外举牌呼吁；一周后的<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日（世界人权日），朱玉芳就被萍乡市警方抓捕，随即被以“寻衅滋事”罪名刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，朱玉芳第二次被萍乡市安源区法院以“寻衅滋事”罪名判刑，这次刑期比上次更长——<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。上诉后，萍乡市中级法院二审裁决维持原判，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。朱玉芳因为被枉法判刑而申诉喊冤，结果却遭到更大打击，被加重判刑。中共当局的司法由此可见一斑。朱玉芳目前在江西省女子监狱四监区服刑。其身患多种疾病，此次又遭受监舍犯人殴打，境况堪忧，亟需关注。朱玉芳在江西省女子监狱的通讯地址：江西省南昌市新建县<span lang="EN-US">916</span>信箱<span lang="EN-US">4</span>分箱（江西省女子监狱四监区）朱玉芳，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">330100</span>，电话：<span lang="EN-US">0791-83718743</span>江西省女子监狱地址：江西省南昌市新建县长堎镇长征路<span lang="EN-US">630</span>号江西省女子监狱。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"></span><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2/</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">杨茂东（郭飞雄）：获刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年的著名人权捍卫者杨茂东（郭飞雄）狱中境况需持续关注<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，本网获悉：一年前的今天，著名人权捍卫者杨茂东（郭飞雄）被以煽动颠覆国家政权罪判处<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年有期徒刑。二审秘密审判，于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日法院驳回郭飞雄的上诉，维持原判。二审后，郭飞雄被转监到广东四会监狱。他在四会监狱中持续绝食，体重掉到<span lang="EN-US">41.5</span>公斤，人已瘦成皮包骨，出现全身发冷，不规则发热，体温在<span lang="EN-US">38</span>摄氏度，最高一次<span lang="EN-US">39</span>摄氏度，经常头晕、站立不稳。检查显示，其患有甲状腺结节，<span lang="EN-US">T3</span>、<span lang="EN-US">T4</span>高；肺部少许炎症；肠息肉，肠道肿瘤标志物增高；肝酶高于<span lang="EN-US">80U/L</span>（正常<span lang="EN-US">40U/L</span>）。郭飞雄狱中健康状况危急，一直强迫鼻饲维持着他的生命。联合国人权专家表示中国政府不能再无视要求释放郭飞雄的呼声，他在狱中的健康状况出现严重恶化。国际社会持续发声与关注让郭飞雄案不会淡出公众视野，是外界挽救郭飞雄生命争取其自由的重要手段。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/05/8.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/05/8.html</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">杨茂东简介：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">笔名郭飞雄，<span lang="EN-US">1966</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日出生，湖北省谷城县人，律师，独立作家，新公民运动和南方街头运动践行者，著名人权活动家，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，曾因申请反对日本右翼的“五四”抗议游行，而被北京市警方以涉嫌“聚众扰乱社会秩序”刑拘<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天；同年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，又因参与广东省南海、佛山、番禺等地的民间维权工作，尤其是参与太石村罢免事件，提供法律援助，并在个人网页上网友通报太石村事件的进展信息，遂于<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日被广州省番禺市警方刑拘，直至<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日才获准释放；<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，高智晟因发起绝食接力活动而被捕，郭飞雄展开营救活动，随即被广东警方以“非法经营罪”刑拘，并遭遇到包括“用电棍击打性生殖器”等方式的刑讯逼供；<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，被广州市检察院正式起诉；同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，被广州市天河区法院以“非法经营罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，并处罚款<span lang="EN-US">4</span>万元。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年，曾因参与组织同年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日<span lang="EN-US">-9</span>日在南方周末集团办公楼前围观声援南方周末职工抗议新年献词被改事件，以及<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，积极组织和促动八大城市街头举牌，敦促全国人大签署《公民权利和政治权利国际公约》活动，而被当局视为是该活动的组织协调者之一，<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日又被广州市天河区警方带走刑拘；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日被转正式逮捕，并被关押在广州市天河区看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，被广州市天河区法院以“众扰乱公共场所秩序罪”、“寻衅滋事罪”重判<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，二审维持原判，后在广东省阳春监狱和英德监狱服刑；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，刑满释放；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月，因其长期流亡美国的妻子张青身患肠癌，生命垂危，随欲赴美予以照顾，熟料却在广州国际机场入关时遭广州警方拦截、失联；获释后，同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，再次赴美时在广州国际机场又被广州市警方以“危害国家安全”为由扣押、失联；其身患晚期癌症的妻子张青终等不到与丈夫见上一面，于美东时间<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日凌晨病逝，身边留下一儿一女；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，被广州市检察院以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”转正式批捕；<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日在广州市中级法院开庭审理，当庭宣判，郭飞雄被判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。其不服判决，上诉。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被驳回上诉，维持原判。此前郭飞雄被羁押于广州市第三看守所。后转监到广东四会监狱。狱中健康状况恶化。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">3/</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陈品霖：遭逮捕的白纸运动《乌鲁木齐中路》纪录片作者陈品霖（网名<span lang="EN-US">Plato</span>）的案情进展：已被起诉到法院<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，本网获悉：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月底被刑事拘留的白纸运动《乌鲁木齐中路》纪录片作者陈品霖（网名<span lang="EN-US">Plato</span>）已于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日被上海市公安局宝山分局以“涉嫌寻衅滋事罪”被正式批捕，于<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日被移送检察院审查起诉。目前其案已于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日由上海市宝山区检察院向上海市宝山区法院提起公诉。陈品霖现被羁押在上海宝山区看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陈品霖简介</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：网名<span lang="EN-US">Plato</span>，白纸运动《乌鲁木齐中路》记录片制作者。生于<span lang="EN-US">1991</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，福建省霞浦县人。在习近平政府推行疯狂清零政策三年期间，中国人民的日常生活和自由遭受到严重的侵害。而新疆乌鲁木齐发生的一场大火彻底将民众对防疫政策的不满点燃。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，当上海人民自发的聚集街头悼念火灾中逝去的同胞时，没人料到这场悼念活动将引发全国范围內对防疫政策的抗议。陈品霖在上海现场拍摄大量视频、制作了《乌鲁木齐中路》纪录片，纪录片再现了民众自发参加悼念乌鲁木齐火灾遇难者，进而演变为要求解封并提出政治诉求的“白纸运动”的过程和场面。陈品霖在白纸运动一周年之际（<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月下旬）将纪录片上传到网络，不到一周，于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，即遭抓捕，而其推特和<span lang="EN-US">Youtube</span>频道被销号。据悉与其一同被抓还有一位女生，后女生获取保，但陈品霖遭遭刑事拘留，后于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日被上海市公安局宝山分局以“涉嫌寻衅滋事罪”被正式批捕，于<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日被移送检察院审查起诉。目前其案已于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日由上海市宝山区检察院向上海市宝山区法院提起公诉。陈品霖现被羁押在上海宝山区看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">4/</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">宋泽：遭抓捕的湖北人权捍卫者<a name="_Hlk167876640">宋泽（本名宋光强）</a>已被起诉<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，本网获悉：于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日被武汉市公安局以“寻衅滋事”罪名刑事拘留的湖北人权捍卫者、中国公民运动参与者宋泽（本名宋光强）于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日被武汉市武昌区检察院提起起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日下午其代理律师在武汉市第二看守所会见了宋泽。宋泽身体状况良好，近期未有遭受虐待。律师已在武昌区检察院阅卷，案卷材料多达<span lang="EN-US">10</span>册，有一米高。宋泽被羁押的罪名十分荒唐，是因涉嫌寻衅滋事罪和提供侵入非法计算机信息系统程序、工具罪。目前羁押在武汉市第二看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/05/blog-post_17.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/05/blog-post_17.html</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">宋泽简介：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">又名宋光强，<span lang="EN-US">1986</span>年生，湖北襄阳人，自称襄阳宋泽。<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>毕业于中南财经政法大学，法学、经济学双学士。公盟负责人、新公民运动的参与者、倡导者。<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年大学毕业后，宋泽曾在一家德资电梯企业武汉的办事处做商务行政事务工作，后又在深圳一家私营评估企业总经理办公室从事助理。<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，宋泽向许志永写信，申请加入公盟，随后以志愿者的身份工作。<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年冬宋泽一直在从事救助访民的工作，给访民捐助物资补给援助，<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年开始了披露和救助被北京黑监狱关押的访民，维权人士。并在两会前期编绘了北京黑监狱地图。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日宋泽因给访民送汤圆而被警方带走，后不久被放出。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，宋泽与赵振甲等十多人冲进湖南郴州驻京办的「黑监狱」，解救出被非法关押的<span lang="EN-US">82</span>岁的龚江保、<span lang="EN-US">73</span>岁的于洪和<span lang="EN-US">57</span>岁的陈碧香等三位上访人士。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日下午<span lang="EN-US">3</span>点宋泽在北京南站等候一位求助者的约见时，被北京公安数位警察强制带走，据宋泽本人描述应该是北京市公安局有预谋的计划。<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，北京市公安局以「寻衅滋事罪」将宋泽刑事拘留<span lang="EN-US">37</span>天，羁押在丰台区看守所。但是期限满时，公安局没有放人，而是将刑拘转为「监视居住」，期限六个月，至<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日到期。许志永认为宋泽被捕是因为救助被关押在黑监狱的三位老人和陈光诚的侄子陈克贵的妻子。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日身为公盟志愿者的宋泽被失踪，后来刘卫国律师偶然发现宋泽被关押在北京市公安局第三拘留所，涉嫌「聚众扰乱社会秩序」罪。宋泽在狱中被赵姓副队长国保殴打，方式为扇耳光、拳打脚踢，无任何人制止。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日宋泽的律师李金星、张磊联名向北京市检察院、最高检察院、公安部等部门提出了就北京市公安局有关警员涉嫌故意伤害、徇私枉法、虐待被监管人犯罪的控告状。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日宋泽由其舅舅到北京为其担保取保候审，在被羁押了<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月零<span lang="EN-US">4</span>天后，走出了北京市第三看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日焦作访民张小玉、许有臣案发生，为了查明真相和声援弱势群体，宋泽等人发起了公民声援团，宋泽提供账户，为张小玉案进行募捐。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日北京警方对道衡律师事务所进行抄家，将余文生律师、王成律师、宋泽、李对龙律师四人抓走。王成律师、李对龙律师不久获释。余文生律师和宋泽遭刑事拘留<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日宋泽被以取保候审的名义获释，结束了<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个多月的羁押，宋泽在押期间一直保持零口供。宋泽（本名宋光强）于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日又被武汉市公安局以“寻衅滋事”罪名刑事拘留，现羁押于武汉市第二看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，在宋泽被抓四个月后，律师在武汉市第二看守所会见了他，被羁押是因涉嫌寻衅滋事罪和提供侵入非法计算机信息系统程序、工具罪。案件已于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日已被武汉市武昌区检察院提起起诉。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">5/</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">邵明亮：江苏省南京市残疾异见人士<a name="_Hlk167877137">邵明亮</a>狱中情况堪忧<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，本网获悉：曾获刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年的江苏省南京市残疾异见人士邵明亮于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日再次被抓捕，羁押至今。现被关押在南京市第二看守所（原鼓楼区、建邺区看守所合并），地址：南京市建邺区下圩村<span lang="EN-US">19</span>号，联系电话<span lang="EN-US"> 02584427947</span>。而家属一直没有收到通知，连衣服都送不进去。南京公民邵明亮，草根出身，民主斗士，多年来遭受南京当局的疯狂报复，被精神病、被车祸致残。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月入狱后四年监禁期间遭受非法虐待，坚决不认罪。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，九死一生出狱后又立即被南京当局非法软禁、不让看病。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，再次被抓捕，羁押至今。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/05/blog-post_44.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/05/blog-post_44.html</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">邵明亮简介：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1967</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日出生，江苏省南京市浦口区人，南京市浦口区江浦街道华光小区响堂村<span lang="EN-US">19-1</span>号居民，残疾异见人士，“中国民复党”创始人，中国政治犯。因反对马列主义而一直高调反共，横遭中共当局的极端打压逼迫，长期被囚禁在响塘村家中，禁止外出购物、就医等；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年，曾因在南京市审计学院门口、浦口区闹市区、浦口区政府前举牌宣传宪政、民主、自由、人权遭警方殴打，后又多次被警方强制送精神病院关押；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，曾在南京浦口区政府门前遭政府默许的车辆辗压全身，导致住院两年，落下终身残疾（盆骨、骶骨、耻骨、肋骨、脊椎、颈椎、胸骨骨折、头、肺、脊骨损伤<span lang="EN-US">)</span>，只能靠轮椅生活；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月、<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，又因反党言论两次被刑拘，其后一直遭家中囚禁；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日<span lang="EN-US">, </span>曾因被搜查住处时，发现室内有“推翻共产主义、社会主义、集体主义三座大山”，“审判毛邓江胡习及其罪犯统治集团首恶分子”等文字，屋外正面墙上写有“民复党纪念八九六四”、“民复党是中国自己的政党”等标语，被南京警方处以行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，中共两会期间，因发反党及嘲讽修宪言论被南京警方处以行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">14</span>天，期间又遭警方暴力殴打；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，再次被南京市浦口区警方抓捕，自此失联；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，被浦口区检察院以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”正式批捕，并被关押在南京市浦口区看守所，指控因其在网上发涉及民主宪政要求的微信和几十条推特内容，所以属于违法行为；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，其案在南京市浦口区法院开庭受审，后被以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年；其不服，表示上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月，经江苏省南京市中级法院二审裁决，依然维持原判，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，邵明亮再次被抓捕，羁押至今。现关押在南京市第二看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">6/</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">谢阳：人权律师谢阳狱中遭酷刑——陈桂秋：谢阳律师案件违法八处<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">谢阳律师在<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">709</span>大抓捕中受尽屈辱和折磨。这次，谢阳律师因维护言论自由又被非法羁押<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年零<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月。我上周与辩护律师沟通，才知道谢阳在看守所里被戴手铐脚链两个星期，并被要求脱光衣服，展示其生殖器，对着摄像头跳艳舞，被要求支付巨额领导约见费。我非常愤怒，便依据谢阳对辩护律师所陈述的，列了<span lang="EN-US">8</span>条长沙市公、检、法、司的违法行为，并对他们违法立案、违法冻结谢阳个人财产、违法审讯谢阳、纵容包庇违法办案人员等违法行为，对涉案单位及涉案人员，将一一对其控告。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/05/blog-post_21.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/05/blog-post_21.html</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">谢阳律师简历</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：<span lang="EN-US">1972</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日出生，湖南省长沙市人，天地人律师事务所和长沙京盈科律师事务所前任律师，原湖南纲维律师事务所律师，人权律师，中国在押政治犯。自<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年正式执业以来，曾因代理多起公权力滥权案件，如山东省曲阜县薛明凯案、北京新公民运动张宝成案、河南省南乐县南乐教案、湖南省浏阳市张开华征地案等维权案件，并积极关注和参与社会维权运动（包括探访盲人律师陈光诚和声援建三江被捕律师等），而屡遭司法当局阻扰和逼迫打压；<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，曾因只身前往山东省东师古村探望盲人律师陈光陈，而被地方黑恶势力殴打抢劫；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，曾因代理一起民间借贷纠纷案，为维护当事人利益要求取得合议庭商议结果，而被湖南省律师协会罚款<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万元，并被所在事务所要求解除合同和离职；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，曾因为“山东薛家命案”作委托代理律师，而被湖南省司法厅当局带走“约谈喝茶”；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，曾因为代理湖南省浏阳市土地维权者张开华案，在出庭时遭到当地法院的野蛮阻扰；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月—<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，因多次代理维权案件，而遭到湖南省律师协会变相打压，不予批准转所手续；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，因其积极代理多起长沙市雨花区强制征地拆迁案件，在代理莲湖村农民征地行政诉讼时，曾遭到当地法院非法驱逐；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，因其代理广西南宁北部湾建材市场当事人的维权案件，曾遭到多名不明身份人员的持械群殴，致其重伤，右腿骨折，其虽报警，但当地警方却迟迟不予出警；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，其在中共“<span lang="EN-US">709</span>大逮捕”中被湖南省长沙市警方抓走，后被以涉嫌“扰乱法庭秩序”、“煽动颠覆国家政权”二罪指定地点监视居住，代理律师要求会见遭拒；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，被长沙市警方以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，其案在湖南省长沙中级法院开庭受审，但因其被迫当庭认罪，否认曾受酷刑，遂于当日暂获取保候审；同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，被长沙市中级法院正式宣判：犯煽动颠覆国家政权罪，但免予刑事处罚；后其虽未被判刑入狱，但仍遭长期软禁和贴身监控；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，谢阳因<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年末前往湖南省永顺县声援因发表网络言论而被强制关进精神病院的怀孕女教师李田田，遂被长沙市警方带走失联，后知被以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”、“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘；其住处遭查抄，许多个人物品均被损毁，两台计算机及一个保险柜被搜走；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，被长沙市检察院以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”予以正式批捕。狱中遭酷刑。目前谢阳律师被羁押于长沙市第一看守所（湖南省长沙市长沙县泉塘街道远大二<span lang="EN-US">1736</span>号，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">410131</span>）。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">7/</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陈翠珠：获刑五年关押在广东省女子监狱广东雷州市法轮功学员陈翠珠被迫害地形同枯木境况堪忧<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，本网获悉：获刑五年关押在广东省女子监狱广东雷州市法轮功学员陈翠珠被迫害地形同枯木，身体境况堪忧。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/05/blog-post_25.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/05/blog-post_25.html</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陈翠珠简介：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">广东省湛江市雷州市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1962</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月生。<span lang="EN-US">1997</span>年开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日晚，陈翠珠因参加集体学法时被湛江市赤坎区警察入屋抓捕，恶警在她家中搜到资料及其辛苦工作积攒下来的现金及存折，声称这是法轮功的经费，企图以此关押构陷。后将她关押在湛江市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日其被警察用手铐脚镣连铐、头脚几乎碰在一起的所谓“庭审”，<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月被湛江市赤坎区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，并罚款<span lang="EN-US">5000</span>元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。判刑后转监至在广东省女子监狱，目前陈翠珠身患重病，身体瘦弱无比、形同枯木，头发掉光，身体状况堪忧。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">8/</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">郝劲松：获刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年的山西著名法律人士郝劲松被转监至山西省太原市第二监狱服刑<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，本网获悉：获刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年的山西著名法律人士郝劲松被转监至山西省太原市第二监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日遭抓捕、后被超期羁押<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>个月的郝劲松于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日被以诈骗罪判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年、寻衅滋事罪判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月，合并执行有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年。其不服上诉，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，山西忻州法院二审维持一审对山西著名法律人士郝劲松诈骗罪、寻衅滋事罪有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年的判决。忻州法院二审没有开庭，采取书面审理形式，终审裁定中没有引述辩护人的意见。而此前郝劲松在看守所内被暴力殴打虐待，家属向有关部门持续控告。目前郝劲松已经被转监至山西省太原市第二监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/05/9.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/05/9.html</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">郝劲松简介：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">生于<span lang="EN-US">1972</span>年，山西忻州人。著名人权捍卫者、法律人。郝劲松自<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年开始先后<span lang="EN-US">7</span>次将国家税务总局、北京地铁运营公司、北京铁路局告上法庭，原他因对“打破行业‘霸王条款’起到了一定作用”而入选“<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年构建经济和谐十大受尊崇人物”。郝劲松被先后提名为<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>中国法制新闻人物，<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年度十大法制人物，并以“维权战士”的身份写入《<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>中国法治蓝皮书》。因介入推动铁道部春运不涨价案件入选《<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>中国法治蓝皮书》，并当选<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>中国十大消费维权人物，<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年因介入陕西华南虎案件和杨佳案被《南方人物周刊》评选为“中国魅力人物——公义之魅”。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年，介入上海“钓鱼执法事件”。后成立山西定襄县劲松法务咨询中心。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年，郝劲松向定襄县环保局实名举报当地的诚泰纺织印染公司涉嫌污染空气和水源。郝劲松于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日、<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日就连续两天遭到户籍地山西省定襄县晋昌镇派出所以“寻衅滋事”为由传唤后，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日再遭该派出所传唤。随后被行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，行政拘留期满被转刑事拘留，控罪为涉嫌寻衅滋事。当日，郝劲松被控涉嫌寻衅滋事遭定襄县公安局刑事拘留。羁押于五台县看守所。案件久不审理，一直拖延至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>至<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日在山西定襄县法院开庭审理。开庭审理一年多后，于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，被超期羁押超过<span lang="EN-US">1200</span>天的著名法律公益人、法律学者郝劲松先生被以诈骗罪判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年、寻衅滋事罪判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月，合并执行有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年。其不服上诉，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日二审驳回上诉，维持原判。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。郝劲松现被转监至山西省太原市第二监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">9/</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">毛善春：遭抓捕的湖北维权人士毛善春取保申请遭拒<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，本网获悉：湖北维权人士毛善春于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日因湖北省两会开幕被迫从武汉回湖北公安县老家过年，于<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日被国保带走，随即关进了看守所，但未给家属任何法律手续。毛善春的老父亲在得知儿子被抓后悲愤交加，已于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日不幸去世。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">近日，湖北省公安县公安局承办人员告知毛善春家属称变更羁押可能有有人身危险性，不同意对毛善春取保。家属认为这也意料之中的事情。毛善春的父亲因为毛被关押自杀身亡，办案人员应该是怕毛善春出来予以报复而不敢释放。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/05/blog-post_59.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/05/blog-post_59.html</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">毛善春简介</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：<span lang="EN-US">1974</span>年生，湖北公民、秦永敏中国人权观察团队成员，籍贯湖北省荆州市公安县章庄铺镇毛家坪村人，曾于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">03</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日公开发表了《关于退出中国共产党的声明》。毛善春于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日因湖北省两会开幕被迫从武汉回湖北公安县老家过年，于<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日被国保带走，随即关进了看守所，但未给家属任何法律手续。毛善春的老父亲在得知儿子被抓后悲愤交加，已于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日不幸去世。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162569632;"></span><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><a name="_Hlk159649535"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">四、</span></b></a></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">本期新增被刑事拘留及强迫失踪的<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人名单及简历<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">：</span></span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">徐琳、池会田、陈合坤<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">徐琳：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1964</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年出生，湖南省株洲市人，诗人，哲学研究者，广东网络作家，独立中文笔会成员，民主异议人士，中国良心犯。自<span lang="EN-US">1990</span>年代末即开始撰写时政文章，诗歌及创作歌曲，至<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年始又在广州，深圳等地积极开展街头举牌，演讲，组织公民集会等活动<span lang="EN-US">;</span>近年来，因与维权公民刘四仿合作，创作并出品了多个以自由，人权，法治为内容的歌曲，颇受自由民主爱好者喜爱与欢迎，遂引起广东当局强烈不满，并成为维稳严控的对象，曾遭多次非法拘禁和秘密关押<span lang="EN-US">;2012</span>年，曾因将浙江异见人士朱虞夫所作诗歌“是时候了”改编谱曲为“就是现在”，引起网友广泛关注和转载而被广州警方于同年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪“刑拘，羁押于广州市番禹看守所，指控其罪行比广州上街举牌还要严重，具有明显煽动群众上街意向，情节十分严重<span lang="EN-US">;</span>后于<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日又被广东省当局改为秘密监视居住它处，期间其家属多次要求当局出示书面通知及关押地点，竟都遭拒<span lang="EN-US">;</span>同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，曾参与民主人士王登朝发起的<span lang="EN-US">'</span>莲花山公园千人公民集会<span lang="EN-US">'</span>，计划于活动现场发表政治演讲，不料事前却遭当局绑架，后被秘密关押<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月<span lang="EN-US">;2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，曾因发布“<span lang="EN-US">709</span>”大抓捕事件而创作的歌曲“正义律师之歌”触怒当局，其任职公司因受当局施压而遭失业，并被绑架至广州软禁<span lang="EN-US">1</span>个月。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，中共<span lang="EN-US">19</span>大召开前夕，其在湖南老家照顾患病父亲时突然被广州市南沙区警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘，其广州住所被查抄，搜走计算机，手机，书籍，笔记本等个人物品；次日，与其一起创作歌曲的搭档刘四方也被江西省宜春市警方以同理由抓走；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，被广州市南沙区检察院以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”正式批捕，关押在广州市南沙区看守所；据悉，被押期间遭酷刑，从<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日—<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日每天都被警方三班倒提讯；一直零口供；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，被广州市南沙区法院以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日。此前其在广东省佛山市高明监狱服刑。徐琳又于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日遭广州市公安局南沙区分局以涉嫌寻衅滋事罪刑事拘留。现羁押在广州市南沙看守所。<b>信息来源：</b></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/05/blog-post_18.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/05/blog-post_18.html</span></b></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">池会田：</span></b></span><a name="_Hlk167881380"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">天主教中国保定教区神父。于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日遭强迫失踪，现音讯皆无，失踪原因不明。河北保定教区神父遭强迫失踪在此地区发生已经不是第一次了。天主教中国河北省保定教区是中国最大的地下<span lang="EN-US">(</span>非官方<span lang="EN-US">)</span>天主教团体之一，该教区因人数众多成为中共当局最为忌讳的教区。针对那些不愿加入中共官方教会机构、不服从中共的神职人员，中共当局经常对其采取“管治”的方式予以强迫失踪来加以整治。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></a></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span _Hlk162448506;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陈合坤：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">12000</span>元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2030</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/05/61.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">海南省琼海市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1971</span>年生。早年修炼法轮功，因坚持法轮功信仰，多次被绑架，曾经三次遭中共公检法构陷、被判刑总计<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年半，期间遭受残暴酷刑。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，邓贤程在贴法轮功标语时，被警察抓捕到定安县龙湖镇派出所，拘留十五天；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，行政拘留期满又被刑事拘留，被转到定安县看守所关押。期间当地公安警察突然非法闯入邓贤程家中进行抄家，掳走私人物品摩托车一辆、手提电脑一台。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月获悉，其最后遭中共当局判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，罚金一万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。目前邓贤程已经被转到海南三江监狱。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/05/6_17.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b New Roman&quot;;">黄礼乔：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">天津市法轮功学员，男，<span lang="EN-US">1966</span>年生，一九八八年大学毕业后，被分配到天津市无缝钢管公司工作。早年修炼法轮功。一九九九年七月中共开始疯狂迫害法轮功后，因黄礼乔坚持修炼法轮功，曾两次遭拘留，三次被劳教，在天津市双口劳教所等处遭受各种酷刑折磨，两次被迫害导致其得上尿毒症。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，黄礼乔再次遭抓捕后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，先后被关押于天津西青监狱、天津滨海监狱，期间被迫害出现肺结核症状。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，天津市公安在黄礼乔出家门时，将他抓捕，随后抄家。黄礼乔随即被关押在河东区看守所。后遭刑事拘留、批捕、起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，黄礼乔被河东区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，罚金一万元。黄礼乔不服判决，上诉至天津市第二中级法院。后被驳回，维持原判。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">黑龙江省哈尔滨市阿城区法轮功学员，男，<span lang="EN-US">1963</span>年。妻子张亚茹：<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，刘洪运、张亚茹夫妇在住处被阿城区国保大队抓捕。刘洪运被关押在阿城区看守所，张亚茹被绑架到哈尔滨第二看守所。期间，刘洪运绝食抗议，于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日取保回家。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，刘洪运又被收监，<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，刘洪运因绝食出现生命危险，被送阿城区医院抢救。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，刘洪运被再次收监。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月获悉：刘洪运、张亚茹夫妇被判刑。张亚茹被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，被关押在哈尔滨市女子监狱，张亚茹刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。刘洪运被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，据说被送到监狱，监狱没收，现被关押在阿城区看守所。刘洪运刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">云南曲靖市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1979</span>年生，云南省曲靖市水电十四局职工，多年前就下岗失业。李红梅曾经于<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，与因为发放真相光盘被抓捕，随后李红梅被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月刑满出狱。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日再次被抓捕，被直接关押到麒麟区看守所。后遭刑事拘留、批捕、起诉。于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日在云南省曲靖市麒麟区法院开庭，随即宣判，李红梅被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">10000</span>元；刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">吉林市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1961</span>年生，家住吉林市丰满区江南乡裕丰馨苑，一九九八年底，雷秀香开始修炼法轮功。一九九九年七月二十日，中共开始疯狂迫害法轮功。从那时起，雷秀香多次被中共抓捕、关押，曾三次被劳教、一次被判刑，在拘留所、洗脑班、看守所、劳教所、监狱遭受迫害，曾经被灌过药、打过毒针、用手铐铐在暖气上、被毒打、电棍电、被扒光衣服，被迫害昏死过一次，遭受百般凌辱折磨。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日晚又被吉林市公安局丰满分局大长屯派出所警察抓捕，关押在吉林市看守所，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月下旬获悉：雷秀香被当地法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，已被转监吉林省女子监狱迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">贵州省贵阳市法轮功学员，男，<span lang="EN-US">1942</span>年生，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">82</span>岁，贵阳市白云区七冶医院退休医生，家住贵阳市白云区长宁社区。于一九九五年开始修炼法轮大法。中共一九九九年七月开始疯狂迫害法轮功后，蒋朝林因坚持真善忍信仰，多年来经常遭中共人员骚扰、绑架，他曾被关进贵州省都云监狱甚至遭酷刑迫害。蒋朝林，曾被劳教两年，被折磨快不行了才送回家。被原单位七冶医院开除工作，生活处于极度困难之中。蒋朝林大约在<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月初被警察抓捕。后获悉其被当地法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，直接将他关押到贵州省都匀监狱。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">吴道芬：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">贵州省贵阳市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1944</span>年生，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">80</span>岁。因坚持修炼法轮大法，经常遭中共人员骚扰、绑架，她曾在贵州省劳教所遭非法劳教迫害。吴道芬曾于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月、<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月、<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月被警察抓捕过，她最后一次被抓捕的具体日期外人不知道，有友人反应自<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月就没见过吴道芬，直到日前路遇吴道芬的妹妹时才知道，吴达芬被当地中共公检法构陷判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，已被关押到贵州省女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/05/46.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">云南曲靖市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1986</span>年生，在昆明工作。徐亚梅曾经于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月因发送法轮功资料而被人举报，后被关押、判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，在云南省第二女子监狱遭受了十一个月的一级严管迫害，直至出狱。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日再次被抓捕，被直接关押到麒麟区看守所。后遭刑事拘留、批捕、起诉。于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日在云南省曲靖市麒麟区法院开庭，随即宣判，徐亚梅被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">8000</span>元；刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">湖北省武汉市法轮功学员，女，一九七三年一月二十六日出生，她原为企业会计，家住武汉市新洲区阳逻街。一九九九年三月，<span lang="EN-US">26</span>岁的周红燕开始修炼法轮功。因修炼法轮功，她曾于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日因在武昌首义学院发放法轮功资料，与其他三名法轮功学员被抓捕。在武汉市第一看守所被关押将近一年后，周红燕于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日被武汉市洪山区法院判刑三年半。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日周红燕女士在武汉某小区发放法轮功资料，被警察抓捕、随即遭关押构陷。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月中旬得知，周红燕已被洪山区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">2</span>日下午，蒋职会正在给百姓发放法轮功资料，遭人举报，被新宾镇派出所警察和国保警察抓捕、抄家。之后，蒋职会被警察刑事拘留、关押在抚顺看守所。后被批捕、起诉。于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，蒋职会被抚顺市顺城区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span bold;">辽宁省锦州市法轮功学员，男，原为葫芦岛人，水泥厂职工。<span lang="EN-US">1957</span>年生，。一九九五年十二月开始修炼法轮功。在这场对法轮功的迫害中，张占安夫妻俩和大儿子多次遭绑架、非法拘留、关洗脑班，多次被罚款，妻子被迫害致死。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，在锦州市古塔公安分局策划下，警察抓捕了张占安等五位锦州法轮功学员。关押到锦州市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，张占安遭凌海市检察院批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月初，张占安被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金七千元。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，被转监到盘锦监狱。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">云南省昆明市法轮功学员，男，<span lang="EN-US">1973</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月出生，家住昆明市西山区，曾做过邮政快递员、网约车司机。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，昆明市金碧派出所几个警察闯进刘志明的家抄家，并将刘志明抓捕，将他关押在昆明市西山区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，刘志明被警察逮捕，之后被构陷到西山区检察院。检察院很快将刘志明构陷到西山区法院。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，云南省昆明市西山区法院开庭庭审法轮功学员刘志明，三天后下达判决，判刘志明<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金一万。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">牛艳：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">（或名牛彦、牛燕）辽宁省本溪市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1951</span>年生。本溪市桓仁县业主沟乡人，她于一九九八年开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年中共当局开始疯狂迫害法轮功，牛彦多次被中共人员抓捕、关押，曾一次被劳教，两次被判刑，累计陷冤狱十一年半。曾在马三家劳教所、辽宁省女子监狱遭受酷刑。牛艳老太太因发放法轮功资料，于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日被本溪市桓仁县公安局国保大队、桓仁派出所警察抓捕，关押在本溪看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月上旬获悉：牛艳被本溪市溪湖区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/05/36_16.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">周洪亮：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">湖北随州法轮功学员，男，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">50</span>岁左右。周洪亮<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日下午在打工的商场，被四个便衣和一个穿制服的警察抓捕、抄家。之后，警察要带走周洪亮。周洪亮拒绝，说：“我要照顾不能自理的<span lang="EN-US">80</span>岁老母亲。”其中四个年轻便衣警察不由分说、上来就用皮带抽打他，当周洪亮往外避让、脱身之时，那四个警察扑上来，追上周洪亮，又是一顿拳打脚踢，凶狠地暴打。随即被关押。后遭刑事拘留、批捕、起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月获悉周洪亮被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，周洪亮被非法关押在随州市看守所<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>个月，于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日被转监湖北沙洋监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/05/36_21.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">梁树发：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">辽宁省锦州市法轮功学员，男，一九五三年生，家住辽宁省锦州市古塔区钟屯乡何屯村。因坚持“真善忍”信仰，他经常遭中共人员骚扰、非法抄家、勒索、非法拘留、关洗脑班等迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，在锦州市古塔公安分局策划下，警察抓捕了梁树发等五位锦州法轮功学员。关押到锦州市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，梁树发遭凌海市检察院批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，凌海市法院在不通知家属的情况下，对梁树发开庭。庭审过程中，梁树发多次高喊“法轮大法好”。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月初，梁树发的家人才听说梁树发已经被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，家属被凌海市法院索要罚金六千元。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，梁树发被转监到盘锦监狱。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年开始修炼法轮功。秦书海因送真相台历，于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日被义县公安局国保、巡特警抓捕。后遭刑事拘留、批捕、起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span bold;">黑龙江哈尔滨市法轮功学员，女，家住哈尔滨市呼兰区康金镇，她是一位善良的农妇。因修炼法轮功，宣讲法轮功，<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，周春玲在呼兰区被抓捕，她后来被判刑十年，在黑龙江省女子监狱遭受背铐、吊铐、戴刑具、上绳、罚蹲等迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日下午四点半左右，周春玲在哈尔滨道外区快餐店工作时，被仁里街派出所警察和呼兰区国保大队警察抓捕。后遭刑事拘留、批捕、起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，周春玲的女儿得知，周春玲被道外区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，罚金一万元。周春玲已经依法提起上诉。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">湖南衡阳市祁东县法轮功学员，。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日和<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，祁东县七名法轮功学员被当地警察抓捕、抄家，他们多数是七、八十岁的老人，包括匡宗尧、邱新乃、唐炳生、张新发等人，随即他们被刑事拘留。后遭批捕、起诉，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月获悉，张新发被判刑<span class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张亚茹：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">黑龙江省哈尔滨市阿城区法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1966</span>年生。丈夫刘洪运，<span lang="EN-US">1963</span>年。夫妻两人早年修炼法轮功，在中共迫害法轮功的二十五年中，刘洪运、张亚茹夫妻因为坚持信仰，屡遭中共绑架、关押、劳教、判刑等迫害，他们的孩子也承受了巨大苦难。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，刘洪运、张亚茹夫妇在住处被阿城区国保大队抓捕。刘洪运被关押在阿城区看守所，张亚茹被绑架到哈尔滨第二看守所。期间，刘洪运绝食抗议，于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日取保回家。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，刘洪运又被收监，<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，刘洪运因绝食出现生命危险，被送阿城区医院抢救。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，刘洪运被再次收监。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月获悉：刘洪运、张亚茹夫妇被判刑。张亚茹被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，被关押在哈尔滨市女子监狱，张亚茹刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。刘洪运被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，据说被送到监狱，监狱没收，现被关押在阿城区看守所。刘洪运刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">山东省济南历城区法轮功学员，男，<span lang="EN-US">1972</span>年生，杨勇因向发放法轮功宣传资料，与<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日被抄家、绑架，被关押构陷一年多后，于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被济南市天桥区法院开庭，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日被警察抓捕，当天下午，将她关押到阳泉市拘留所行政拘留十五天。<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，李桂林被刑事拘留，关押到阳泉市看守所。后又遭批捕、起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日被庭审，律师依法辩护，要求无罪释放。但平定县法院不顾法律与事实，对她判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，李小凤结束三年半冤狱回家。仅仅三年后，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日上午，张德国去凌海市石山镇大集发法轮功宣传资料，被石山镇派出所警察抓捕抄家，警察抄走法轮功书籍、优盘等物品。张德国随即被关押到凌海看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">35/</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">廉晶：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">辽宁沈阳法轮功学员，男，<span lang="EN-US">1950</span>年生，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">74</span>岁，辽宁地矿测绘院的退休职工，家住沈阳市沈北新区。早年修炼法轮功，在中共对法轮功迫害的二十五年中，亷晶坚持修炼，曾被劳教<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年半和判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。廉晶老先生<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，被沈阳市公安局铁西分局警察抓捕；后遭刑事拘留、批捕、起诉，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月初获悉，廉晶被当地法院判<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚款五千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/05/7416.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/05/7416.html</span></b></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">36/</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">徐丽秀：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">湖北省黄冈市浠水县法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1966</span>年生。黄冈市浠水县洲瓦镇铜锣山村人，她常年在武汉市武昌区徐家棚地区以打零工为生。一九九九年前，徐丽秀修炼法轮功。徐丽秀因坚持修炼，多次被中共绑架、关押，曾被劳教、判刑，在看守所、劳教所、洗脑班、监狱遭受多次酷刑迫害。徐丽秀<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，在武汉市武昌区徐家棚地区，被抓捕关押到武汉洗脑班后，五个多月杳无音信。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月中旬获悉，徐丽秀被秘密判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，现被关押在湖北省洪山监狱。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">湖北省随州市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1950</span>年生。家州住随市万店镇。龙泽清<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月被人举报，未抓捕被立案。后于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日遭庭审、没宣判，当日回家。后龙泽清被判刑一年，监外执行。立案已经一年时间过去了，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，龙泽清被抓捕，随即关押到湖北沙洋范家台监狱迫害。抓捕人员说又给她加期半年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" lang="EN-US">20</span>日早上，罗美林被九江市柴桑区警方抓捕，随即遭刑事拘留、批捕、起诉。后罗美林被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，目前，她被关押在九江市看守所，她将被留在看守所坐牢役，直到她的刑期结束。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">C</span>、<span lang="EN-US">D</span>、<span lang="EN-US">E</span>、<span lang="EN-US">F.....X</span>、<span lang="EN-US">Y</span>、<span lang="EN-US">Z</span>）。查询者可依据姓名的第一个拼音字母，即可查询到相关人员姓名，而其简介均可在报告中查找到。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span
